\quad\texttt{StepXILocalTermCThetaAudit}.
\end{array}
\]
Here the Proposition~1.4/1.5 estimates are produced from local analytic
construction sources: distinguished and nondistinguished finite-extension
Haar/log-volume log-shell constructions, and archimedean direct-sum metric
constructions.  The strict route has also been lowered to the additive-Haar
version of this boundary:
\[
\begin{array}{l}
\texttt{strictFiniteToyOneSidedIUTIVTheorem110AdditiveHaarLocalAnalytic}\\
\quad\texttt{ArithmeticDivisorStepXILocalTermCThetaSource},\\
\texttt{StrictFiniteToyOneSidedIUTIVTheorem110AdditiveHaarLocalAnalytic}\\
\quad\texttt{ArithmeticDivisorStepXILocalTermCThetaAudit}.
\end{array}
\]
This audit exposes the actual additive Haar compact-open normalization
endpoint at each distinguished and nondistinguished finite place, then projects
to the local-analytic strict audit.  Thus the strict finite diagnostic no
longer stops at generic finite-extension log-shell data before entering the
Step~(xi) \(C_\Theta\) comparison.

The Step~(x) record names the finite-divisor packet, realified Frobenioid
log-Kummer source, Kummer/forgetting compatibility, vertical-\(IQ\) target
source, and packet source-target log-volume calibration.  Its constructor
from the typed indeterminacy core proves the equality/equality/inequality
pattern: \((\Ind_1)\) and \((\Ind_2)\) preserve procession-normalized
log-volume, while \((\Ind_3)\) only gives a one-sided bound.  The same
Step~(x) record now carries the relation-level
\texttt{Ind3UpperSemiRelationAudit}, so this one-sided law remains a named
certificate in the paper-trace obligations rather than merely an extracted
function field.  The paper-trace API now also exposes projections for the
typed Theorem~3.11 action-law audit, the relation-level \((\Ind_3)\)
upper-semi audit, the step-level \((\Ind_3)\) transport certificate, and the
fact that \((\Ind_3)\) contributes no generator to the equality quotient.  The
Step~(xi)
record names the remaining Remark~3.9.5 hull/determinant work: holomorphic hull
operator, possible-image family matching, q-region containment, Ob1/Ob2 hull
absorption, Ob3/Ob4 determinant normalization, Ob5 quotient compatibility, Ob7
prime-strip retention, tensor-power bound, and the q-region-to-theta
log-volume chain.  In the current top-level audit, the tensor-power slot is the
constructed normalized determinant bound, while the q-region slot is the
separate inequality obtained by composing q-to-determinant and determinant-to-
theta in the constructed record bridge.

The IUT~IV record names the local-to-global \(C_\Theta\) obligations below the
current additive-Haar boundary: Proposition~1.4 distinguished log-shell
inclusions, now instantiated as per-place arithmetic-divisor-backed component
endpoints; Proposition~1.4 numerical bounds, now instantiated as the local
different/conductor nonnegativity facts; the nondistinguished zero log-volume
result, now instantiated as the per-place nondistinguished additive-Haar
log-shell endpoint; Proposition~1.5 metric containment, now instantiated as
the per-place archimedean metric endpoint; the Theorem~1.10
arithmetic-divisor source; distinguished and archimedean formula-to-gap
comparisons, now instantiated as named per-place comparison endpoints;
additive Haar local normalization; the Step~(xi)-to-IUT~IV local
matching equality; the finite-place arithmetic gap
\(C_{\Theta,\mathrm{can}}+1\leq A_{\mathrm{upper}}-M_{\log}\); and the global
proof of \(C_{\Theta,\mathrm{can}}\leq C_\Theta\).  Its
\texttt{LocalToGlobalArithmeticChainAudit} now has named projections for all
seven chain entries, including the local Step~(xi)-to-IUT~IV arithmetic-term
matching, the finite-place arithmetic gap, and the final
\(C_{\Theta,\mathrm{can}}\leq C_\Theta\) comparison.

The trace now also has a separate preferred-boundary record,
\texttt{AdditiveHaarArithmeticDegreePadicObligations}.  This names the
remaining constructions specifically used by the deepest current additive-Haar
endpoint: Theorem~1.10 additive-Haar local analytic construction, local
arithmetic matching, arithmetic-divisor formula splitting, \(p\)-adic
prime-error/defect/main-log splitting, Step~(xi) arithmetic-degree

identifications, determinant-multiplicity and adjusted-log-volume identifications,

Hodge/\(\SHE\)/\(\IPL\) provenance now threaded through that endpoint.  Its
\texttt{RemainingPayloadAudit} is included in the assembled corridor audit, so
the preferred route no longer hides these lower source assumptions behind the
generic IUT~IV \(C_\Theta\) record.  Each component also has a named Lean
projection theorem.  This makes the next source-math work precise: the local
analytic additive-Haar construction, arithmetic-divisor splitting,
\(p\)-adic error decomposition, Step~(xi) arithmetic-degree calibration, and
the determinant/log-volume identifications must be constructed individually
before this audit can be discharged.

The assembled
\texttt{Obligations} record adds the endpoint-level requirements that the final
preferred theorem must not expose either the raw
\(\theta_{\mathrm{signed}}\leq C_\Theta(-q_{\mathrm{signed}})\) input or the
raw \(C_{\Theta,\mathrm{can}}\leq C_\Theta\) comparison as public hypotheses.
From the assembled \texttt{RemainingPayloadAudit}, Lean now reconstructs the

Its Theorem~3.11/remarks subledger now also contains a
\texttt{typed\_indeterminacy\_nonvacuity\_witness\_constructed} slot,
discharged at the strongest current boundary by the strict two-point typed

\section{Next Work}

The remaining mathematical work is organized by the trace audit above.  One
major branch is still to construct, rather than assume, more of the
source-facing \SHE{} and Hodge-descent preservation data.  The route is:
\[
\begin{array}{c}
q^{j^2}\text{ finite Gaussian endpoint with pivotal restriction}\\
\Downarrow\\
\text{Gaussian and splitting monoid construction}\\
\Downarrow\\
\text{factored square/full-label preservation}\\
\Downarrow\\
\text{Hodge/SHE transport audit}\\
\Downarrow\\
\text{hull/log-volume comparison}\\
\Downarrow\\
C_\Theta\ge -1 .
\end{array}
\]
The project should continue by replacing the present record fields for
factored \SHE{} preservation and Hodge-descent source-target alignment with
the corresponding constructions from \IUT{} I--III.
The first source-derived bridge layer has now been added: the final
finite-divisor vertical-\(IQ\) route can consume separated \(\IPL\),
\(\SHE\), hull/determinant, and theta/Hodge calibration source components
instead of an opaque route-alignment argument.  The \(\SHE\) component has been
refined to a finite Hodge/SHE transport package that exposes the two theater
sides, the finite label equivalence, full-label log-volume preservation,
transported-average preservation, and the current history-separation guard.
It now also has a typed source boundary that carries the Hodge-theater descent
bridge and a typed allowed-forgetting witness separately from the
synchronization-derived finite preservation data.  The remaining work is to
make each of those components itself follow from the relevant source-paper
constructions, rather than supplying them as records.
The \(\IPL\) component can now be constructed at the public finite-divisor
vertical-\(IQ\) endpoint from the finite Hodge/\(\SHE\) transport together with
a Theorem 3.11 IPL-link construction source.  The endpoint no longer receives a
free-standing \(\IPL\) datum, source/target endpoint equalities, or a separate
\(\IPL\) log-volume transport source: the constructed input-prime-strip link
gives the endpoint equalities definitionally, the source object aligns that
constructed datum with the pre-ledger certificate, and log-volume preservation
is read from the finite Hodge/\(\SHE\) transport.
The foundational qualitative certificate is no longer only a nonempty
bookkeeping triple.  The declarations
\[
\begin{array}{l}
\texttt{HodgeTheaterTransportSystem},\\
\texttt{StructuredSHETransportContext},\\
\texttt{AlgorithmicParallelTransportConstruction}
\end{array}
\]
record permitted Hodge-theater transport arrows, forbidden theater
identifications, and APT data built from a permitted arrow.  Lean proves that a
forbidden domain-to-codomain SHE identification admits no allowed transport
arrow, and that the constructed APT datum has the permitted arrow's mechanism,
the constructed output family, the output-family equality back to the
pre-ledger family, the allowedness proof, and the resulting non-forbiddenness
of the APT arrow.  The Stage~1 wrapper
\(\texttt{ConstructedQualitativeCertificateData}\) pins the pre-ledger
certificate to the certificate constructed from these IPL/SHE/APT objects and
returns both a compact qualitative transport audit and this stricter APT
transport audit.
The finite Hodge/\(\SHE\) transport layer now has the corresponding source
discipline audit
\[
\begin{array}{l}
\texttt{IUTStage1ConstructedQualitativeFiniteHodge}\\
\quad\texttt{SHETransportDisciplineAudit}.
\end{array}
\]
It records, in one object, that the finite Hodge/\(\SHE\) comparison uses only
the history-separated forgetful reading, while the constructed \(\SHE\)
transport system forbids a direct domain-to-codomain identification and the
\(\APT\) arrow is separately proved non-forbidden.  Thus the finite comparison
is no longer documented merely by a side inequality; the typed
allowed/forbidden transport discipline is visible next to it.
The route-facing constructor
\[
\texttt{IUTStage1ConstructedQualitativeFiniteHodgeSHETransportSource}
\]
now packages this as source data: from the constructed qualitative bundle and
the Hodge--Arakelov theta evaluation synchronization, it builds the
history-separated finite Hodge/\(\SHE\) transport source and returns the same
typed discipline audit.  In particular, the finite forgetful comparison is
kept separate from the forbidden direct \(\SHE\) identification while the
permitted \(\APT\) arrow remains part of the constructed qualitative input.
The next bridge,
\[
\texttt{IUTStage1ConstructedQualitativeFiniteHodgeSHEIPLConstructionSource},
\]
adds the constructed Theorem~3.11 \(\IPL\) link to this same source object and
projects to the existing finite Hodge/\(\SHE\)+\(\IPL\) log-volume chain.  Thus
the \(\IPL\) handoff can now be audited from the constructed qualitative
\(\SHE/\APT\) transport boundary through the constructed input-prime-strip
link, with no separate finite Hodge/\(\SHE\) source supplied at that layer.
This is the present typed replacement for the older raw
\(\texttt{HasStructuredIPL/SHE/APT}\) certificate fields.  The Theorem~3.11
source layer now exposes
\(\texttt{IUTStage1Theorem311ConstructedQualitativeInputs}\): its pre-ledger
audit is induced from the constructed qualitative certificate, it projects back
to the existing structured-input route, and it exposes the forbidden
SHE-domain-to-codomain transport guard together with the permitted APT
non-forbiddenness proof.  This has now been promoted to the strengthened SHE
route surface by
\(\texttt{IUTStage1Theorem311ConstructedQualitativeInputsWithSHE}\), which
projects to the existing \(\texttt{StructuredInputsWithSHE}\) route, builds the

Corollary~3.12 audit constructors without asking callers to supply a raw
pre-ledger audit.  The same constructed boundary now reaches the named
Theorem~3.11-to-Corollary~3.12 checkpoint layer:

There is now also a certificate-pinned variant of this boundary.  It reads the

hull, that union agrees with both the Theorem~3.11 record and the package
target union, the tensor-power determinant bound supplies the
\(\theta_{\mathrm{signed}}\) bound, and the constructed hull/determinant source

control, and the raw \(q_{\mathrm{signed}}\le\theta_{\mathrm{signed}}\)
comparison.  This gives reviewers a Step (xi)-native audit target before the
finite-divisor route projects it into the later vertical-\(IQ\) corridor.

boundary is used for compatibility.  The direct \(C_\Theta\) audit computes the

Remark~3.11.2 also treats the mono-analytic \(\pm\)-procession index sets as
naked finite sets, not as further arithmetic holomorphic data.  Lean now models
the component indexed by \(j\) as \(\mathrm{Fin}(j+1)\), proves that any finite
type of cardinality \(j+1\) is equivalent to this chosen model, and packages the
family of choices
\[
\prod_{j=0}^{l} \mathrm{Fin}(j+1).
\]
The total cardinality is proved to be \((l+1)!\), matching the paper's
\(l^{\pm}!\) count.  This audit is attached to the absolute-label procession
source, so the formal passage to \(\pm\)-processions now records both the
quotient of labels and the naked mono-analytic counting data.

This source is canonical: \texttt{ofCoordinate} builds the full-label family from
a log-theta coordinate, \texttt{ofChoice} attaches it to a concrete
Hodge-theater/log-theta choice, and
\texttt{ConcreteHodgeTheaterLogThetaFullLabelProcessionSource.canonical}
assembles the choice-wise family for the whole concrete source space.

now tied to the source-level no-omission statement constructed from the

\[
  C_{\Theta,\mathrm{can},v}+\delta_v
    \leq
  A_v-M_v .
\]
Lean proves
\[
  C_{\Theta,\mathrm{can}}+1
    \leq
  \mathrm{arithmeticUpperTerm}-\mathrm{mainLogTerm}
\]
by summing these local inequalities with
\(\texttt{Finset.sum\_le\_sum}\), using the equalities
\[
  C_{\Theta,\mathrm{can}}=\sum_v C_{\Theta,\mathrm{can},v},\qquad
  \mathrm{arithmeticUpperTerm}=\sum_v A_v,\qquad
  \mathrm{mainLogTerm}=\sum_v M_v,
\]
and the finite-divisor/Haar normalization condition
\[
  1\leq\sum_v \delta_v .
\]

  S_v+\delta_v\leq A_v-M_v,\qquad S_v\leq A_v-M_v,

arithmetic-degree term, together with the construction of the underlying local
log-shell and metric estimates.

certificate-pinned declarations are retained only as review aliases until they

passes from the generated full-label kernel-image q-region source to the
local-normalization valuation-ball source before invoking the finite-divisor
\(C_\Theta\) corridor.  The q-region side has now been lowered once more by
\[
\begin{gathered}
\texttt{concreteHodgeTheaterLogThetaGeneratedFullLabel}\\
\texttt{FiberInd2ActionPacketTransportGeneratedCorridor}\\
\texttt{KernelImagePullbackLocalNormalization}\\
\texttt{MatchedValuationBallFactoredLocalized}\\
\texttt{HullCoverUpperRayCalibrationSource\_}\\
\texttt{cThetaDichotomy}.
\end{gathered}
\]
This endpoint consumes the generated-corridor-backed q-region source directly,
derives the pointwise q-region route internally, and retains both the
generated-corridor audit and the target-region quotient audit at the
local-normalization valuation-ball \(C_\Theta\) boundary.  Two further lowered
endpoints now remove the generated-corridor source from the public boundary:
\[
\begin{gathered}
\texttt{concreteHodgeTheaterLogThetaGeneratedFullLabel}\\
\texttt{LatticeImageLawGeneratedQuotientLocalNormalization}\\
\texttt{MatchedValuationBallFactoredLocalized}\\
\texttt{HullCoverUpperRayCalibrationSource\_}\\
\texttt{cThetaDichotomy}.
\end{gathered}
\]
At this boundary Lean derives the generated-corridor q-region source from the
lattice-image-law generated quotient attached to the concrete fiber transport.
This has now been lowered further.  The current lowest packet-level
\(C_\Theta\) boundary is
\[
\begin{gathered}
\texttt{concreteHodgeTheaterLogThetaGeneratedFullLabel}\\
\texttt{FiberInd2ActionPacketTransportPointwiseGeneratedPullback}\\
\texttt{DirectLocalNormalization}\\
\texttt{ValuationBallFactoredLocalized}\\
\texttt{HullCoverUpperRayCalibrationSource\_}\\
\texttt{cThetaDichotomy}.
\end{gathered}
\]
The public q-region payload is now the pointwise Theorem~3.11 record-image
pullback to the concrete fiber-lattice theta-class image law.  The generated
target-region pullback is derived from this law using the record realization of
possible images as comparison target regions.  Lean then proves the
\((\Ind1,\Ind2)\)-quotient compatibility of the target-region family, constructs
the equality-quotient possible images, and derives the representative
target-region, common-kernel, kernel-image, generated-record, q-region, and
generated-corridor handoffs internally.  The endpoint still takes the
Remark~3.9.5 local-normalization valuation-ball/Haar hull-cover source directly.
That valuation-ball input is now audited at the same boundary by
\[
\texttt{directLocalNormalizationValuationCoverAudit}.
\]
The audit exposes the common finite-extension degrees and compact-open Haar
masses for the matched concrete/generated local factors, the derived raw
degree/Haar equalities, and the localized vector-bundle component transport
used by the upper-ray calibration.
The generated quotient evidence is now exposed at two adjacent boundaries.  At
the generated-corridor/local-normalization boundary it is recorded by
\[
\begin{gathered}
\texttt{generatedCorridorLocalNormalization}\\
\texttt{ValuationCoverQuotientHullAudit}.
\end{gathered}
\]
This uses the generated full-label quotient corridor itself, before the
finite-divisor \(C_\Theta\) handoff, to identify the selected q-region as a
selected \((\Ind1,\Ind2)\)-quotient possible image and to prove its containment
in the Remark~3.9.5 canonical hull.  At the pointwise/direct boundary the same
evidence is recovered after reconstructing the generated corridor, via
\[
\begin{gathered}
\texttt{generatedFullLabelValuationCoverQuotientHullAudit}.
\end{gathered}
\]
The direct boundary now also retains the concrete finite-label procession:
\[
\begin{gathered}
\texttt{generatedFullLabelConcreteProcession}\\
\texttt{ValuationCoverQuotientHullAudit}.
\end{gathered}
\]
For every \(F_\ell\)-label over the selected theta class, Lean proves the
generated choice has the selected Remark~3.9.5 possible region, the same hull
log-volume as the selected \(q\)-choice, and the same theta-class pullback
region.  Thus the no-omission full-label check remains visible after the
pointwise/direct local-normalization step.  At the valuation-cover level, this
audit has now been pushed through the generated-record and target-region
boundaries.  From the generated record-image pullback law, Lean reconstructs
the pointwise q-region source and the generated full-label quotient corridor;
from the target-region/common-kernel source, it derives the
\((\Ind1,\Ind2)\)-quotient family.  In both cases the source itself carries the
selected quotient/hull audit and the concrete \(F_\ell\)-procession audit.  The
quotient target-region boundary goes one step lower still: its q-side payload
is already a target-region family on the equality quotient, together with the
pullback to generated full-labels and the representative theta-class
calibration to the concrete fiber-lattice image law.  The remaining
source-facing obligation is therefore sharper: construct the target-region and
quotient target-region comparisons, together with the valuation-cover
local-normalization witnesses, from the same local log-Kummer/Frobenioid
geometry.
The older factored localized hull-cover source
\[
\begin{gathered}
\texttt{ConcreteHodgeTheaterLogThetaGeneratedFullLabel}\\
\texttt{FactoredLocalizedHullCoverUpperRayCalibrationSource}.
\end{gathered}
\]
is now an intermediate projection from the valuation-ball factored boundary
\[
\begin{gathered}
\texttt{ConcreteHodgeTheaterLogThetaGeneratedFullLabel}\\
\texttt{ValuationBallFactoredLocalizedHullCoverUpperRayCalibrationSource}.
\end{gathered}
\]
This earlier valuation-ball boundary remains an intermediate interface: it
retains the concrete/generated upper-ray objects, the theta-class q-region
calibration, the common hull system, and the hull/determinant identifications,
but obtains both localized hull-cover sources and their component transport from
matched valuation-ball Haar covers.

The practical priority order is now:
\begin{enumerate}
\item Construct the source-side witnesses for the generated-full-label to
  finite-divisor vertical-\(IQ\) handoff.  The handoff record, record-image,
  theta-class, finite-packet projection, and constructed finite-packet
  theta-class sources are now implemented.  The target-region realization is
  derived from the finite Theorem~3.11 record image, and the selected
  record-image witness is derived from an \((\Ind1,\Ind2)\)-backed fiberwise
  audited-packet representative finite theta-class image law.  The signed
  package transfer is no longer a bare equality field at the review boundary:
  it is derived from constructed Step~(xi) upper-ray q-region, q-pilot, and
  theta-hull comparisons; on the concrete/generated side, those q/theta
  comparisons have now been factored through q-region plus hull-operator
  calibration and finite adjusted determinant summand matching.  What remains
  is to construct the audited packet
  representatives, the same-theta-class
  midpoint packet, the ordered \((\Ind1)\) procession leg, the source-level
  nonarchimedean \(\mathrm{Ism}\) action leg, the raw tensor-label equations,
  the target summand-kind certificate, and the remaining q-region,
  hull-operator, and adjusted determinant-summand matching witnesses from
  paper-native finite divisors, local objects, and log-volume comparison data.
\item Construct the finite divisor-component columns--local object, prime
  multiplicities, prime degrees, and unit log-volume--and construct the
  labelled vertical object-transport records from the paper-native vertical
  log-Kummer correspondences.  The current Lean boundary constructs the
  Frobenioid degree object from these components, derives the finite degree-sum
  law definitionally, derives the labelled compatibility equality from the
  object transports, constructs the ordinary realified divisor column, then
  constructs the normalized theta and log-shell Example~3.5 copies, derives
  log-shell normalization and divisor realization, proves raw vertical
  translation, and upgrades object transport to full labelled local-object
  identity.
\item Construct the component functions below the theta-pilot representative
  section from the same log-Kummer/log-link geometry.  The current \Lean{}
  boundary builds the representative section from class-wise finite labels,
  procession states, local tensor states, and upper-semi non-volume data, then
  inserts the Frobenioid base-volume compatibility datum and derives the old
  calibration equalities, the one-sided \((\Ind3)\) base-volume inequality, the
  ordinary-copy comparison, finite local log-shell objects, base
  finite-log-volume equalities, column log-link transport family, and the
  transported \(ZMod(\ell)\), capsule, classified, and direct bridges.  The
  newest kernel separates this from the ambient choice-space assumption by
  generating the canonical theta-pilot choices themselves.  It has now been
  strengthened to generate the entire finite \(F_\ell\)-label procession over
  each theta-pilot class, with the \(Z/\ell Z\)-action closed internally,
  projected to the ambient \texttt{flProcessionTranslate}, and routed through
  Step~(xi), Remark~3.9.5, and the current global \(C_\Theta\) audit.  The
  remaining source-construction work is to derive the component functions from
  the paper-native local geometry.
\item Migrate or retire older certificate-pinned \(\IPL\) review aliases that
  are no longer preferred source surfaces.
\item Extend the recovered finite-divisor packet-local source from the
  preferred constructed-\(\IPL\) record-hull boundary to any remaining older
  vertical-\(IQ\) review aliases, and construct the deeper
  log-Kummer/Frobenioid packet calibrations of \IUT{} III, Step~(x), rather
  than accepting them as source-facing packet-boundary fields.
\item Construct the remaining Step~(xi) holomorphic-hull/determinant fields
  from Remark~3.9.5 and Step~(xi): genuine hulls, determinant lines,
  Ob5/Ob7 compatibility, and the \(\theta_{\mathrm{signed}}\) log-volume
  identification.  The preferred principal local boundary now defines the
  local log-shell as the selected compact-open factor and has a realized-exact
  boundary \(P_{\Theta,\beta}=\operatorname{real}_\beta(U_\beta)\) from which
  \Lean{} derives compact-open coordinates, image containments, realized
  valuation-ball equality, the exact \(\Xi(P_B)\) source, and the
  source-derived global \(C_\Theta\) audit.  This has now been pushed lower in
  two directions.  Valuation-ball realized exactness plus the valuation-ball
  additive Haar audit recovers the compact-open realized-exact source used by
  the preferred audit.  Equivalently, the two compact-open image containments
  construct the compact-open realized-exact source directly, recover the
  broader equality-backed log-shell source from four local
  image/valuation-ball containments, define the canonical local log-Kummer
  graph as the graph of the realization map, and now construct the map-level
  possible-region source by taking the Kummer map to be the valuation-factor
  realization and choosing its section from canonical graph left-totality.  In
  the reverse direction, that possible-region map source now constructs the
  theta-region graph source by the principal-cover equality
  \(P_{\mathrm{cover}}(\Theta)=P_\Theta\), and then reaches pointwise
  valuation-ball exactness and log-shell exactness.  The
  image containments are also derived from a cover-level exactness statement
  identifying the selected Remark~3.9.5 possible region with the realized
  compact-open local factor, and now from the lower log-shell exact source
  \(P_{\Theta,\beta}=\operatorname{real}_\beta(L_\beta)\),
  \(L_\beta=U_\beta\).  These exact equalities are themselves derived from the
  pointwise local realization source, which is now derived from compact-open
  local-chart data and from the compact-open log-Kummer graph source.  The
  theta-region-defined Step~(xi) valuation cover is now also constructed from
  the source-core Remark~3.9.5 valuation-ball/Haar cover using the
  fiber-transport-backed pointwise comparison, and from the lattice-image law
  once it is identified with the fiber-transport source, to derive the
  cover/theta-region family equality; in the fiber-derived case this
  identification is now checked definitionally.  What remains is to construct
  the fiber-transport comparison, the identification for any independently
  supplied lattice law, and the graph/local-chart laws from the paper-native
  holomorphic hull, log-Kummer, and local log-shell geometry.
\item Instantiate the valuation-ball local analytic construction from actual
  local fields, log-shell maps, compact-open Haar normalizations, and
  archimedean lattice metrics, proving the remaining Proposition~1.4
  log-shell estimates and Proposition~1.5 metric containments below those
  objects.
\item Complete the finite-extension residue/Haar layer below the current
  boundary: construct the residue field action on \(\mathcal O[K_v]\), prove
  that \(p_v\mathcal O[K_v]\) is a residue submodule, and derive the
  coset/Haar-character formula for genuine finite extensions rather than only
  for the base \(p\)-adic field and abstract finite-extension source records.
\item Derive the point-level target transport for the principal finite-divisor
  regions \(O\) and \(\lambda O\), including positive valuation-ball radius,
  coordinate-place equivalence, local scalar-image laws, direct-product
  localization covers, and the chart/direct-summand log-volume calibrations.
\item Instantiate the typed \IUT{} IV arithmetic-divisor source from actual
  number-field valuations, the different, \(q\)-parameter, and conductor
  divisors, and prove the distinguished and archimedean formula-to-gap bounds
  from the local analytic construction rather than carrying them as route
  payloads.
\item Extend the Hodge--Arakelov theta-evaluation wrapper beyond the current
  finite degree-evaluation, bad-local quotient, canonical-label, and
  canonical-one synchronization shadows toward the Gaussian/Frobenioid
  constructions of \IUT{} II and the Hodge-theater descent bridge.
\item Only then evaluate whether the Stage~1 interface has enough source
  content to bear on the Mochizuki--Scholze--Stix disagreement.
\end{enumerate}
